 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&#160;9, 2021, iCAD, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the quarter ended September&#160;30, 2021. A copy of the Company&#8217;s press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. Exhibit 99.1 is being furnished pursuant to Item 2.02, is not to be considered filed under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), and shall not be incorporated by reference into any of the Company&#8217;s previous or future filings under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) Exhibits </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="right">


<IMG SRC="g928183snap0001.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ICAD REPORTS FINANCIAL RESULTS FOR THE QUARTER ENDED SEPTEMBER&nbsp;30, 2021 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>- Third Quarter Revenues of $9.4 Million Represented 20% Sequential Quarter Growth over the Second </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Quarter of 2021, Driven by 26% Growth in Detection Revenue and 10% Growth in Therapy Revenue &#150; </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>- Third Quarter 2021 Revenues Represented 31% Growth Compared to the Third Quarter 2020 &#150; </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>- Improving Enterprise Sales in the Third Quarter of 2021 Resulted in a 41% Sequential Quarter </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Increase in Detection Product Revenues &#150; </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>- Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP>Product Revenue
Reflected a 34% Sequential Quarter Increase in the Third Quarter of </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>2021 with Continued Surge in Dermatology Controller
Installations - </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>- Company to Host Conference Call&nbsp;&amp; Webcast today at 4:30 PM ET </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NASHUA, N.H. &#150; November</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;9, 2021 &#150;</B> <U>iCAD, Inc</U>. (NASDAQ: ICAD),&nbsp;a global medical technology leader providing
innovative cancer detection and therapy solutions, today reported its financial and operating results for the three and nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenues for the three-month and nine-month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 were $9.4&nbsp;million and $25.8&nbsp;million, respectively, compared to
$7.1&nbsp;million and $19.2&nbsp;million in the three and nine month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2020, respectively. This represents 31% growth over the third quarter 2020 and 20% growth over the second quarter 2021. Net loss for the
three-month and nine-month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2021, were $2.2&nbsp;million and $7.1&nbsp;million, respectively, compared to $1.8&nbsp;million and $16.0&nbsp;million in the three and nine-month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2020,
respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recent Highlights: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Experienced continued market demand for ProFound AI<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>
Risk, the first and only commercially available clinical decision support tool providing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-year</FONT> breast cancer risk estimation personalized for each woman, in the U.S. and Europe, with improving enterprise
sales in the third quarter resulting in a 41% increase in sequential quarter Detection product revenues, with U.S. product sales increasing 56% compared to last quarter </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Launched ProFound AI<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Risk (3D mammography), alongside
an enhanced version of PowerLook<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Density Assessment. These technologies provide critical, risk-adaptive solutions for clinicians facing complex screening challenges when personalizing
wellness assessments regardless of a patient&#146;s ethnicity </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Continued commercial focus in the Therapy business drove $3.4&nbsp;million in revenues, which represents a 10%
increase in sequential quarter revenues, supported by the ongoing demand for dermatology controller installations, which continues to benefit from favorable market conditions from both a regulatory and reimbursement standpoint </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Increased portfolio of clinical evidence around iCAD&#146;s
Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> brain intraoperative radiation therapy (IORT) with new data presented at American Association of Neurological Surgeons demonstrating significant improvement in overall survival in
recurrent glioblastoma patients after treatment </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">98 Spit Brook Road, Suite 100 Nashua, NH 03062 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">phone: 603.882.5200 toll free: 866.280.2239 fax: 603.218.6658 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">www.icadmed.com </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="right">


<IMG SRC="g928183snap0001.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our third quarter total revenue of $9.4&nbsp;million, which represented a 20% increase over last
quarter, and a 31% increase over the third quarter of 2020, was our third highest quarterly revenue total since 2018. Importantly, despite the continued impact from a slightly elongated sales cycle which emerged last quarter, we saw a recovery in
Detection sales momentum in the third quarter of 2021, driven by sequential quarter and year-over-year third quarter increases in product revenues of 41% and 15%, respectively. Looking ahead, we expect this product sales growth to continue with the
recent commercial launch of our new 3D Risk assessment offering, which provides superior insights that empower clinicians to tailor a woman&#146;s breast screening regimen and potentially identify cancers earlier,&#148; said Mike Klein, Chairman and
CEO. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Moreover, we continued to experience significant growth in our Therapy business in the third quarter of 2021, as we generated sequential
quarter and year-over-year third quarter increases in Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> product revenues of 34% and 188%, respectively. This momentum is being driven by an ongoing surge in dermatology controller
installations, propelled by the emergence of positive shifts in reimbursement, payor coverage and regulatory changes. Our Xoft brain IORT application represents a key catalyst for our Therapy segment, and we continue to generate compelling data
supporting its efficacy and expect to treat the first patients in our GLIOX clinical trial later this month,&#148; Mr.&nbsp;Klein added. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Third Quarter
2021 Financial Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the third quarter of 2021 was $9.4&nbsp;million, an increase of $2.2&nbsp;million, or
31%, as compared to the third quarter of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue: Cancer Detection revenue for the third quarter of 2021, which includes the Company&#146;s
mammography and breast density products, and the associated service and supplies revenue, increased by approximately $0.7&nbsp;million, or 14%, to $6.0&nbsp;million, as compared to the third quarter of 2020. Therapy revenue for the third quarter of
2021, which includes Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Axxent<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> eBx<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> System<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> sales, as well as the associated service and supplies revenue, increased by $1.5&nbsp;million, or 82%, to $3.4&nbsp;million, as compared to the third quarter of 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

compared to $13.9&nbsp;million, or 72% of revenue, in the same period in 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the nine months ended
September&nbsp;30, 2021 were $25.1&nbsp;million, a $3.3&nbsp;million, or 15.3%, increase from $21.8&nbsp;million in the same period in 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net
Loss: Net loss for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2021, was ($7.1) million, or ($0.29) per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($16.0) million, or ($0.73) per diluted share, for the same period in 2020. GAAP Net Loss in 2020
included a $7.5&nbsp;million charge related to the losses on fair value of convertible debentures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>
Adjusted Net Loss: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the first nine months of 2021 was ($6.6) million, or ($0.27) per
diluted share, as compared to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss of ($8.1) million, or ($0.37) per diluted share, for the first nine months of 2020. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the nine-month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 and 2020, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA, a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the first nine months of 2021 was ($3.9) million, a $0.9&nbsp;million decrease as compared to the first nine months 2020
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA of ($4.8) million. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148;
and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA results for the nine-month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 and
2020, respectively. </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="right">


<IMG SRC="g928183snap0001.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company reports its financial results in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles, or GAAP. However,
management believes that in order to understand the Company&#146;s short-term and long-term financial and operational trends, investors may wish to consider the impact of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, when used as a supplement to financial performance measures in accordance with GAAP. These items result from facts and circumstances that vary in frequency and/or impact on continuing
operations. Management also uses results of operations before such items to evaluate the operating performance of the Company and compare it against past periods, make operating decisions, and serve as a basis for strategic planning. These <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide management with additional means to understand and evaluate the operating results and trends in the Company&#146;s ongoing business by eliminating certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses and other items that management believes might otherwise make comparisons of the Company&#146;s ongoing business with prior periods more difficult, obscure trends in ongoing operations or reduce
management&#146;s ability to make useful forecasts. Management believes that these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide additional means of evaluating period-over-period operating performance. In addition,
management understands that some investors and financial analysts find this information helpful in analyzing the Company&#146;s financial and operational performance and comparing this performance to its peers and competitors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management defines <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA&#148; as the sum of GAAP Net Loss before provisions for interest
expense, other income, stock-based compensation expense, depreciation and amortization, tax expense, severance, gain on sale of assets, loss on disposal of assets, acquisition and litigation related expenses. Management considers this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to be an indicator of the Company&#146;s operational strength and performance of its business and a good measure of its historical operating trends, in particular the extent to which
ongoing operations impact the Company&#146;s overall financial performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures do
not replace the presentation of the Company&#146;s GAAP financial results and should only be used as a supplement to, not as a substitute for, the Company&#146;s financial results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company has provided a
reconciliation of each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure used in its financial reporting and investor presentations to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management excludes each of the items identified below from the applicable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure referenced above
for the reasons set forth with respect to that excluded item: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Interest expense: The Company excludes interest expense which includes interest from the facility agreement,
interest on capital leases and interest on the convertible debentures from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA calculation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Stock-based compensation expense: excluded as these are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses
that management does not consider part of ongoing operating results when assessing the performance of the Company&#146;s business, and also because the total amount of expense is partially outside of the Company&#146;s control as it is based on
factors such as stock price volatility and interest rates, which may be unrelated to our performance during the period in which the expense is incurred. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Tax Expense: The Company excludes this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> item from the 2020
periods as it was not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations. In January 2021, the Company adopted ASU <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2019-12</FONT> requiring these taxes be moved to operating expenses and are no longer excluded. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">CARES Act Credit: The Company excludes this item as it is related to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> legislation that does not have a direct correlation to future business operations, as this item was in direct response to the initial wave of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
pandemic. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Severance and Furlough: The Company excludes this item as it is related to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> business impact that does not have a direct correlation to future business operations, as this item was in direct response to the initial wave of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
pandemic. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Amortization and Depreciation: Purchased assets and intangibles are amortized over a period of several years and
generally cannot be changed or influenced by management after they are acquired. Accordingly, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items are not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that
such expenses do not have a direct correlation to future business operations. Thus, including such charges does not accurately reflect the performance of the Company&#146;s ongoing operations for the period in which such charges are incurred.
